DETECTOR   (HPGE) An Al frame was installed for twelve HPGe       23073  1   39 
           detectors. Four detectors may be supported at each of  23073  1   40 
           110, 125 and 150 deg angles. First eight detectors were23073  1   41 
           currently placed at 110 and 150 deg -four in horizontal23073  1   42 
           and four in vertical plane. Seven detectors have       23073  1   43 
           relative efficiency of 100 % and one - 70%.            23073  1   44 
            Detection efficiency was measured with Eu152 point    23073  1   45 
           source.                                                23073  1   46 
            Also MCNP simulations to determine efficiency         23073  1   47 
           corresponding to the extended dimensions of sample.    23073  1   48 
           (FISCH)  U-235 fission chamber at 200 m cabin - to     23073  1   49 
            monitor neutron flux, for absolute normalization.     23073  1   50 
MONITOR    (92-U-235(N,F),,SIG) All measurements relative to      23073  1   51

ANALYSIS   The total neutron inelastic cross section were         23073  4   15 
           calculated from the gamma production cross sections    23073  4   16 
           in energy range 862-4500keV  by formula:               23073  4   17 
           SIG(tot.inl)=1.000*SIG(847)+0.031*SIG(1811)+           23073  4   18 
           0.022*SIG(2113)+0.048*SIG(2273)+0.170*SIG(2523)+       23073  4   19 
           1.000*SIG(3448)+0.350*SIG(2983) ,                      23073  4   20 
           where SIG(###) - gamma production cross section for    23073  4   21 
           gamma energy ### keV.                                  23073  4   22 
           The level sequence, the placement of the gamma         23073  4   23 
           transitions, and the branching ratios were taken from  23073  4   24 
           REL-REF of H.Junde+.                                   23073  4   25 
REL-REF    (R,,H.Junde+,J,NDS,112,1513,2011)                      23073  4   26 
COVARIANCE  Correlation ( between energy points) matrix for total 23073  4   27 
           inelastic cross section is on Fig.2 of                 23073  4   28 
           PR/C,90,034602,2014.                                   23073  4   29 
ERR-ANALYS Uncertainties introducing correlations between various 23073  4   30 
           cross sections determined in this experiment:          23073  4   31 
           (ERR-1) Uncertainty from the activity of the source    23073  4   32 
           used for efficiency calibration of the HPGe detectors: 23073  4   33 
           0.7%; common for all detectors;                        23073  4   34 
           (ERR-2) Uncertainty from the beam monitoring with the  23073  4   35 
           fission chamber - 1.5 %.                               23073  4   36 
           (ERR-S) The statistical uncertainty of the HPGe data is23073  4   37 
           of the order of 2% for each detector for the strongest 23073  4   38 
           neutron energy channels. This is reduced by the fact   23073  4   39 
           that eight detectors were used. Further, if the        23073  4   40 
           statistical uncertainty remains too high, authors group23073  4   41 
           a few time channels adding the statistics and          23073  4   42 
           sacrificing time resolution.                           23073  4   43 
           (ERR-T) Total uncertainty includes all sources of      23073  4   44 
           errors for the strongest channels - 5-6% .             23073  4   45 
COMMENT    Of author.                                             23073  4   46 
           The total cross section is precise up to the energy of 23073  4   47 
           the last observed level. Beyond this energy it         23073  4   48 
           represents only a lower limit of the real inelastic    23073  4   49 
           cross section. However, this limit is very close to the23073  4   50 
           real value because most of the gamma decay of 56Fe     23073  4   51 
           proceeds through the first excited level 846.8 keV, 2+ 23073  4   52 
           and the decay of this level is clearly observed.       23073  4   53

           that detectors were used. Further, if the statistical  23073  8   28
